Phase 6 (Implementation Plan §Phase 6). Mirrors Descriptive Study
Plan.md §7 (Steps 1-10) and §9 (visualization plan) section-for-section,
and `scripts/run_cascade.py`'s data-loading logic, so this report stays
auditable against both documents line by line.
&#10;Item 2 ("wire report sections to cascade.py/trends.py/viz.py") is done:
every Step section below calls the real Phase 4 (`cascade.py`/
`trends.py`) and Phase 5 (`viz.py`) functions directly -- no numbers are
hand-typed into this file. Where Phase 5 has a dedicated chart/table
renderer (Steps 1, 2, 6, 9, 10) it is used; where it does not (Steps 3,
4, 5, 7, 8) the step's table is shown as a markdown table via this
file's own `show_table`/`show_tableone` helpers, the same convention
`scripts/run_cascade.py` already uses for its markdown report.
&#10;Item 4 (self-describing header) is also done: "Report metadata" prints
the analysis date, the data snapshot's own last-modified date, the
pipeline's git commit hash (`+dirty` if the working tree has
uncommitted changes), and record count, then shows every Sec 6 QC
rule's row counts in/out (`qc.run_qc(raw).summary` -- aggregate counts
only, never the record-level `flagged` table).
&#10;Parameters follow Quarto's Jupyter/Papermill convention: override at
render time with, e.g.
    quarto render report/descriptive_report.qmd -P as_of:2026-07-01
-->

## Report metadata

    Analysis date (as_of): 2026-06-16
    Data snapshot: 2026-06-16 (VladKovMur_dataset.csv)
    Pipeline commit: d1e6015+dirty
    Records (n): 7732

*QC rule row counts (Descriptive Study Plan §6): `n_checked` is the
denominator the rule applied to (excludes not-applicable records),
`n_violations` is how many of those failed it. Run against the raw input
prior to any derived-variable transforms; see `reports/qc_report.md` for
the full per-site QC appendix.*

| rule                         | n_checked | n_violations | violation_rate |
|:-----------------------------|----------:|-------------:|---------------:|
| duplicate_registration       |      7732 |           18 |     0.00232799 |
| treatgroup_onehot            |      7732 |           30 |     0.00387998 |
| outcome_mutual_exclusivity   |      1214 |            0 |              0 |
| date_order                   |      7628 |         2030 |       0.266125 |
| doses_taken_le_schema        |      1155 |          126 |       0.109091 |
| dose_threshold_consistency   |      7732 |          126 |      0.0162959 |
| diagnosis_mutual_exclusivity |      7705 |            0 |              0 |
| age_range                    |      7676 |            1 |    0.000130276 |

All counts and percentages below have small cells (n \< 5) suppressed
per Descriptive Study Plan §11. No row-level identifiers (`Source_id`,
`Nomer`, `IndexCase`) appear in this report — `Source` site-name labels
appear only as an aggregate stratification dimension.

## Step 1 — Population profile (Table 1)

Frequencies/percentages of `Source`, `TargetGroup`, `Sex`, age band, and
`RelationWithSource` (contacts), overall and by site; median/IQR for age
and contacts screened per `IndexCase`.

## Step 2 — Screening cascade

Proportion screened → suspected TB → Diaskintest positive → fully
evaluated, for the full cohort and by `TargetGroup`/site.

## Step 7 — Incentive payment uptake

Proportion receiving each incentive among those eligible, and median
delay between milestone and payment date; compared by site.

*Uptake by incentive (% of each incentive’s own eligible cohort)*

| incentive  |    n | count |      pct |   ci_low |  ci_high | suppressed |
|:-----------|-----:|------:|---------:|---------:|---------:|:-----------|
| screening  | 4618 |  4150 | 0.898657 | 0.889619 | 0.907033 | False      |

var x = new MutationObserver(function (mutations, observer) {{
        var display = window.getComputedStyle(gd).display;

var x = new MutationObserver(function (mutations, observer) {{
        var display = window.getComputedStyle(gd).display;
        if (!display || display === 'none') {{
            console.log([gd, 'removed!']);
            Plotly.purge(gd);
            observer.disconnect();
        }}
}});

    x.observe(notebookContainer, {childList: true});
}}

    x.observe(outputEl, {childList: true});

## Limitations

Per Descriptive Study Plan §10: right-censoring (records enrolled close
to the analysis date cannot yet show a mature outcome); programmatic,
non-randomized data (site/target-group differences may reflect
implementation rather than treatment effects — no causal inference is
intended); structural (not data-quality) missingness for fields that
only apply to certain target groups; outcome ascertainment depends on
follow-up completeness, which may vary by site.
